|                Name                |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            Versions                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |                                                             Description                                                             |
|------------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `client_connection_check_interval` | [14](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-14#client_connection_check_interval), [15](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-15#client_connection_check_interval), [16](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-16#client_connection_check_interval), [17](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-17#client_connection_check_interval)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             | Sets the time interval between checks for disconnection while running queries.|
| `tcp_keepalives_count`             | [11](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-11#tcp_keepalives_count), [12](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-12#tcp_keepalives_count), [13](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-13#tcp_keepalives_count), [14](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-14#tcp_keepalives_count), [15](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-15#tcp_keepalives_count), [16](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-16#tcp_keepalives_count), [17](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-17#tcp_keepalives_count)                      | Specifies the number of TCP keepalives that can be lost before the server's connection to the client is considered dead.|
| `tcp_keepalives_idle`              | [11](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-11#tcp_keepalives_idle), [12](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-12#tcp_keepalives_idle), [13](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-13#tcp_keepalives_idle), [14](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-14#tcp_keepalives_idle), [15](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-15#tcp_keepalives_idle), [16](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-16#tcp_keepalives_idle), [17](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-17#tcp_keepalives_idle)                             | Specifies the number of seconds of inactivity after which TCP should send a keepalive message to the client.|
| `tcp_keepalives_interval`          | [11](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-11#tcp_keepalives_interval), [12](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-12#tcp_keepalives_interval), [13](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-13#tcp_keepalives_interval), [14](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-14#tcp_keepalives_interval), [15](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-15#tcp_keepalives_interval), [16](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-16#tcp_keepalives_interval), [17](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-17#tcp_keepalives_interval) | Specifies the number of seconds after which a TCP keepalive message that is not acknowledged by the client should be retransmitted.|
| `tcp_user_timeout`                 | [12](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-12#tcp_user_timeout), [13](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-13#tcp_user_timeout), [14](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-14#tcp_user_timeout), [15](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-15#tcp_user_timeout), [16](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-16#tcp_user_timeout), [17](../server-parameters-table-connections-and-authentication---tcp-settings.md?pivots=postgresql-17#tcp_user_timeout)                                                                                                                                                                           | Specifies the amount of time that transmitted data may remain unacknowledged before the TCP connection is forcibly closed.|

### Reporting and Logging / When to Log



|              Name               |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   Versions                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |                                                               Description                                                               |
|---------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `log_min_duration_sample`       | [13](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-13#log_min_duration_sample), [14](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-14#log_min_duration_sample), [15](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-15#log_min_duration_sample), [16](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-16#log_min_duration_sample), [17](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-17#log_min_duration_sample)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  | Sets the minimum execution time above which a sample of statements will be logged. Sampling is determined by log_statement_sample_rate.|
| `log_min_duration_statement`    | [11](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-11#log_min_duration_statement), [12](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-12#log_min_duration_statement), [13](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-13#log_min_duration_statement), [14](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-14#log_min_duration_statement), [15](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-15#log_min_duration_statement), [16](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-16#log_min_duration_statement), [17](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-17#log_min_duration_statement) | Sets the minimum execution time (in milliseconds) above which statements will be logged. -1 disables logging statement durations.|
| `log_min_error_statement`       | [11](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-11#log_min_error_statement), [12](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-12#log_min_error_statement), [13](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-13#log_min_error_statement), [14](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-14#log_min_error_statement), [15](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-15#log_min_error_statement), [16](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-16#log_min_error_statement), [17](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-17#log_min_error_statement)                      | Causes all statements generating error at or above this level to be logged.|
| `log_min_messages`              | [11](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-11#log_min_messages), [12](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-12#log_min_messages), [13](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-13#log_min_messages), [14](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-14#log_min_messages), [15](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-15#log_min_messages), [16](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-16#log_min_messages), [17](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-17#log_min_messages)                                                                       | Controls which message levels are written to the server log.|
| `log_startup_progress_interval` | [15](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-15#log_startup_progress_interval), [16](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-16#log_startup_progress_interval), [17](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-17#log_startup_progress_interval)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            | Time between progress updates for long-running startup operations.|
| `log_statement_sample_rate`     | [13](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-13#log_statement_sample_rate), [14](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-14#log_statement_sample_rate), [15](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-15#log_statement_sample_rate), [16](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-16#log_statement_sample_rate), [17](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-17#log_statement_sample_rate)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        | Fraction of statements exceeding log_min_duration_sample to be logged.|
| `log_transaction_sample_rate`   | [12](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-12#log_transaction_sample_rate), [13](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-13#log_transaction_sample_rate), [14](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-14#log_transaction_sample_rate), [15](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-15#log_transaction_sample_rate), [16](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-16#log_transaction_sample_rate), [17](../server-parameters-table-reporting-and-logging---when-to-log.md?pivots=postgresql-17#log_transaction_sample_rate)                                                                                                                    | Sets the fraction of transactions from which to log all statements.|

|           Name            |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     Versions                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |                                                                               Description                                                                                |
|---------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `bgwriter_delay`          | [11](../server-parameters-table-resource-usage---background-writer.md?pivots=postgresql-11#bgwriter_delay), [12](../server-parameters-table-resource-usage---background-writer.md?pivots=postgresql-12#bgwriter_delay), [13](../server-parameters-table-resource-usage---background-writer.md?pivots=postgresql-13#bgwriter_delay), [14](../server-parameters-table-resource-usage---background-writer.md?pivots=postgresql-14#bgwriter_delay), [15](../server-parameters-table-resource-usage---background-writer.md?pivots=postgresql-15#bgwriter_delay), [16](../server-parameters-table-resource-usage---background-writer.md?pivots=postgresql-16#bgwriter_delay), [17](../server-parameters-table-resource-usage---background-writer.md?pivots=postgresql-17#bgwriter_delay)                                                                | Specifies the delay between activity rounds for the background writer. In each round the writer issues writes for some number of dirty buffers.|

| `bgwriter_lru_maxpages`   | [11](../server-parameters-table-resource-usage---background-writer.md?pivots=postgresql-11#bgwriter_lru_maxpages), [12](../server-parameters-table-resource-usage---background-writer.md?pivots=postgresql-12#bgwriter_lru_maxpages), [13](../server-parameters-table-resource-usage---background-writer.md?pivots=postgresql-13#bgwriter_lru_maxpages), [14](../server-parameters-table-resource-usage---background-writer.md?pivots=postgresql-14#bgwriter_lru_maxpages), [15](../server-parameters-table-resource-usage---background-writer.md?pivots=postgresql-15#bgwriter_lru_maxpages), [16](../server-parameters-table-resource-usage---background-writer.md?pivots=postgresql-16#bgwriter_lru_maxpages), [17](../server-parameters-table-resource-usage---background-writer.md?pivots=postgresql-17#bgwriter_lru_maxpages)               | In each round, no more than this many buffers will be written by the background writer.|
| `bgwriter_lru_multiplier` | [11](../server-parameters-table-resource-usage---background-writer.md?pivots=postgresql-11#bgwriter_lru_multiplier), [12](../server-parameters-table-resource-usage---background-writer.md?pivots=postgresql-12#bgwriter_lru_multiplier), [13](../server-parameters-table-resource-usage---background-writer.md?pivots=postgresql-13#bgwriter_lru_multiplier), [14](../server-parameters-table-resource-usage---background-writer.md?pivots=postgresql-14#bgwriter_lru_multiplier), [15](../server-parameters-table-resource-usage---background-writer.md?pivots=postgresql-15#bgwriter_lru_multiplier), [16](../server-parameters-table-resource-usage---background-writer.md?pivots=postgresql-16#bgwriter_lru_multiplier), [17](../server-parameters-table-resource-usage---background-writer.md?pivots=postgresql-17#bgwriter_lru_multiplier) | The average recent need of buffers is multiplied by bgwriter_lru_multiplier to arrive at an estimate of the number of buffers that will be needed during the next round.|

### Write-Ahead Log / Archive Recovery



|           Name            |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           Versions                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |                                 Description                                  |
|---------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
